I have a 1953 house with the main heat source a wall heater in the living room. <name>David Bullock</name><Text>We recently had a jammed Badger 0.5HP In-sink-erator unit and called Any-Tyme out to assist.

He ignored the fact that it was still making a very audible humming noise, nor did he try loosening the stuck blade or using an Allen wrench to dislodge the blockage.

When my wife asked me if it was OK (I was in the other room working), I told her no.  Cesar immediately countered that Any-Tyme did not want to lose our business and asked "How much would you be willing to pay?" and when my wife was confused, he immediately dropped his quote to $300.00 to replace the unit and started waffling about whether the unit could be made to work again or needed replacing.  He kept pressing but I told my wife to stand firm.

Thinking it was an isolated case of a dishonest and predatory technician, I called the dispatcher at the company -- they proudly claim to be family owned so I thought they would want to know. I asked for another quote, and she indicated that she had no price book and took my number to have their head person call me back.

I was disappointed that they made no effort to call me back and remedy the situation.  I've told me wife that we're not to consider using them in the future, and let our neighbors know to beware if they should find themselves dealing with Any-Tyme.

After talking to some family about this, at their suggestion I went out and bought a $1.30 1/4" Allen Wrench at Ace Hardware and was able to free to blockage in the disposal in 2 minutes by inserting it into the bottom of the unit and turning it both directions.  It's now working fine again.  No burned out motor, no new unit, no ripoff.</Text>< rating>

Easy to reserve a truck. However, we could not get the size we wanted for a local move. The $19 a day enclosed truck can not be rented locally, only for out of town rentals. We did not need a 15 foot truck and a pickup or van was not large enough. We did rent a 15 foot $29 a day truck because we did have to move some items and it seemed to be our only option. The trucks handle well. They have a dolly and packing blankets inside the back that you can choose to rent by cutting the plastic ties if you need those items. The dolly is very small though. < review>
The gentleman who runs this place is a terrific guy. Just really friendly and willing to help. It's a boutique shop, specializing in wood and wind mostly, I think. So I would call first to make sure they have the items or services you need (you won't find any Marshall Stacks in there). I needed help with some wiring on my active pups, and that's not really the kind of work he does here. But if he can't help you, he'll recommend someone who can. He recommended Arnie, over at Klines on Sutterville, and Arnie fixed the active EMG's on my electric guitar for $20.<//review>

The service was good and friendly.  The Coco Taro slush and Avocado smoothie tasted good but didn't wow us.  The boba was slightly firm.  The macarons seem to have a buttercream filling.  Their baked goods near the cashier had no prices listed when I went.  I got the brown butter chocolate chip ($2.50) and it did taste good but seemed a little underdone.  I grabbed their ube blueberry scone ($3.00) and this just killed it for me.  This didn't taste good at all to me.  I tasted no ube or blueberry.  What I did taste was so overpowering. < Review>
It seems impossible to say but here it goes.... these are the best macarons ( NOT macaroons ) I have had in the states, PERIOD. perfectly chewy shell, a little salty a little sweet, theyre INCREDIBLE. I tried about 10 different flavors so far and I could never say enough amazing things about them to do them justice, TRY THEM! Better than "Honey and Butter", better than "Le Macaron" and slightly larger than Honey and Butter and way larger than Le Macaron! Pride and passion went into these perfect Macarons! Incredible selection of flavors as well!
Also the service was amazing. Above and beyond friendly and helpful. Hard to believe a place this 5 star still exists today! Thanks to the cute and sweet girls that helped us!
Their boba is very good, cooked properly, good flavor. Nice and chewy, not over cooked not undercooked. VERY GOOD! I ordered Honey Jasmin Green tea, it was not too sweet like so many other places.
Massive selection of teas, desserts, toppings, etc. They even have salted cheese foam which is super delicious!
I will drive to SD SPECIFICALLY to come to this place. Do yourself a favor and try this place!</Review>

<review>Good place to get your tea/milk tea cravings fulfilled. They have your standard drink "toppings", e.g., boba, small boba, pudding, etc...but they also have white boba which is a bit sweeter. They advertise their Thai tea as being "slow brewed", but I couldn't really taste a significant difference. They advertise that it's creamier, but to me it tasted smoother/silkier: as if they used milk as opposed to creamer. Not a bad thing - I liked it that way.

Also, one thing I enjoy about this place is their courtesy. All the times I have gotten a drink, upon receiving it they have told me, essentially, that if my drink isn't up to my standards to let them know and they will re-do my drink. Also their drinks are labeled like...I guess the best way to put it is like a Starbucks drink, i.e., you know and they know and any person will know what the drink is.

<username>Brianne Livas</username><Date>1587238496065<//Date>< Rate>

< review>
Small Mom and Pop sushi joint, but they never disappoint. We tend to go for lunch. Never a wait for a table, rolls always come out quickly (yet properly and tasty). Not my go to for all-you-can-eat simply because they don't offer as many appetizers or the teriyaki chicken like other places.... but for Sushi by the roll I haven't found a better place yet.

I highly recommend the 38. Burrito Special Roll to anyone looking for something a little different. My go-to rolls also include the 29. B.S. II Roll, 50. Golden Tiger Roll, 47. Dragon Roll and 35. Crunch Roll. I've tried many others as well and all are great.

Also great for take out!!< /review>

<text>Update to prior review:

To be fair I will say that this is my 2nd time using extra space storage at this location specifically, because the location is convenient, easy to manage, and has OnSite management. My first experience was good. Not many complaints except the office hours should be extended at least until 7pm for the people that work a 9-5 or 9-6pm shift.

This brings me to my current experience: Lesea the store manager was helpful and nice the first day I moved into storage 11/12/2016. So much so that she gave me some furniture coverings that she personally had with no charge. I gave her a review with 5 stars that day. Since then however her customer service has gone out the door! She is rude and short on the phone (opposite of face to face service). She doesn't practice "active listening" but rather argue back and forth until you let her have the last word. I've been behind on a few payments and simply called in to make an arrangement to bring things up to date. I explained I can make it in today  by closing at 6pm. Lesea yelled continuously that she has a surgery and will be going out of town, and that I need to be there by 5:45 in order to be helped. I explained that I'll be traveling from Antioch and will call by 5:45pm when I arrive nearby. Lesea argued for a good 3-5 minutes that I am not hearing her clearly and that she will not help me after 5:45 because she has to go out of town. (Sounds like a personal matter) If your store hours are until 6pm why would you refuse service 15minutes before. I'm out done with the way she has  handled things lately. It's always personal with her, as if she owns the company or location. I will be moving my things out sooner than later. All I want to do is make a payment and sign paperwork.
